                - EFFICIENT BATTERY USAGE/OpenGL Technology!
                <br/>
                Custom built and native coded, this live wallpaper is optimized for very low battery usage! Created using OpenGLES, you will get the most fluid, most battery-optimized experience for your phone.
                <br/>
                - INTERACTIVE/Touch the screen!
                <br/>
                This Live Wallpaper comes with multiple touch events.
                <br/>
                By touching the screen, you will create a beautiful particle splash. Try swiping left and right the leave behind an awesome trail of particles and you can tap to interact with all the different elements.
                <br/>
                - CUSTOMIZABLE/Change the effects!
                <br/>
                You can increase the size, speed or density of the elements, as well as select three different color effects. Just open the app, click on "Set Live Wallpaper" and then click on "Settings"
                <br/>
                - HD GRAPHICS/Unique design!
                <br/>
                The design of this live wallpaper is 100% unique, created by our team of artists. You will not see any similar design in any other live wallpapers!
                <br/>
                We have tested this live wallpaper on a multitude of Android phones. If you have any problems using this live wallpaper, please send us an email at mangoappst@gmail.com and we will assist you right away! We're eager to chat and receive your feedback!
